dadebuli xelSekrulebis baTilad cnoba 1\2 wilze.

bul qorwinebaSi mopasuxe _ i. wiklaurTan. erTad cxovrebis period-


Si, 1997 wels, maT SeiZines TbilisSi, ... mdebare #65 bina, romelic aRi-


ricxa i. wiklauris saxelze. kanonis Tanaxmad, bina warmoadgens meuR-

mesakuTred cnoba. man, agreTve, moiTxova 2003w. 22 maiss i. wiklaursa


da i. WeliZes Soris dadebuli am binis nasyidobis xelSekrulebis ba-


Tilad cnoba 1\2 wilze, im safuZvliT, rom binis naxevari mis sakuTre-


bas warmoadgens da i. wiklaurs ar hqonda ufleba, gaesxvisebina igi.

bris gadawyvetilebiT i. botkovelis sarCeli dakmayofilda nawi-

kuTred, rasac safuZvlad daedo is garemoeba, rom sadavo bina SeZe-


nilia meuRleTa erTad cxovrebis periodSi da warmoadgens maT saer-

dadebis gamo bina ver aRiricxa myidvelis _ i. WeliZis saxelze da am-

Tbilisis saolqo sasamarTlos saapelacio palatis 2004w. 17 mai-


sis ganCinebiT saapelacio saCivari ar dakmayofilda, ucvlelad


darCa raionuli sasamarTlos gadawyvetileba.


saapelacio palatam ganmarta udavoa, rom i. wiklauri da i. botko-


veli daqorwindnen 1995 wels, xolo 1997 wels i. wiklaurma SeiZina


TbilisSi, ... mdebare #65-e bina, romelic Tbilisis teqnikuri aRric-


xvis samsaxurSi gaformda mis saxelze.sk-is 1158-e muxlis pirveli na-


wilis Tanaxmad, meuRleTa mier qorwinebis ganmavlobaSi SeZenili qo-


neba warmoadgens maT saerTo sakuTrebas (TanasakuTrebas), Tu maT So-


ris saqorwino xelSekrulebiT sxva ram ar aris dadgenili. amdenad,


sadavo bina unda CaiTvalos meuRleebis: i. botkovelisa da i. wiklau-


ris saerTo sakuTrebad da imis gaTvaliswinebiT, rom gadawyvetile-


bis gamotanis momentisaTvis igi teqbiuroSi jer kidev aRricxuli


iyo i. wiklaurze (binaze yadaRis dadebis gamo), sasamarTlom savsebiT


marTebulad aRiara i. botkoveli am binis TanamesakuTred.


saapelacio palatam ar gaiziara i. wiklauris mosazreba imis Sesa-


xeb, rom bina SeZenilia misi mSoblebis mier. palatis miTiTebiT, teq-


nikuri aRricxvis samsaxuris monacemebiT, bina aRricxuli iyo i. wik-


lauris da ara misi mSoblebis saxelze, xolo sk-is 312-e muxlis pir-


veli nawilis Tanaxmad, sajaro reestris monacemebis mimarT moqme-


debs utyuarobisa da sisworis prezumfcia, e.i. reestris monacemebi


iTvleba swored, vidre ar damtkicdeba maTi uzustoba. amdenad, vid-


re ar dadasturdeba sawinaaRmdego, binis myidvelad da mis mesakuT-


red miCneul unda iqnes i. wiklauri da ara misi mSoblebi. amasTan, sk-


is 1158-e muxlis Tanaxmad, i. botkoveli miCneul unda iqnes i. wikla-


uris saxelze ricxuli binis 1\2-is mesakuTred.

imaze, moaswro Tu ara myidvelma aRricxva sajaro reestrSi am nivTis

dakmayofilebaze uaris Tqmis nawilSi da am nawilSi miRebul iqnes


axali gadawyvetileba botkovelis sarCelis dakmayofilebis Sesaxeb. 


samotivacio nawili:


palatam Seiswavla saqmis masalebi, moismina mxareTa ganmartebebi


da mivida daskvnamde, rom gasaCivrebuli ganCineba unda gauqmdes da


saqme xelaxla gansaxilvelad daubrundes saapelacio palatas Sem-


deg garemoebaTa gamo:


ssk-is 394-e muxlis Tanaxmad, gadawyvetileba yovelTvis CaiTvleba


kanonis darRveviT miRebulad, Tu gadawyvetileba iuridiulad ar


aris sakmaod dasabuTebuli an dasabuTeba imdenad arasrulia, rom ga-


dawyvetilebis samarTlebrivi safuZvlianobis Semowmeba SeuZlebelia.


ssk-is 249-e muxlis meoTxe nawilis Tanaxmad, gadawyvetilebis sa-


motivacio nawilSi unda aRiniSnos sasamarTlos mier dadgenili ga-


remoebani, mtkicebulebani, romlebsac emyareba sasamarTlos das-


kvnebi, mosazrebani, romlebiTac sasamarTlo xelmZRvanelobda.


amave muxlis me-5 nawilis Tanaxmad, gadawyvetilebis sarezolu-


cio nawili unda Seicavdes sasamarTlos daskvnas sarCelis dakmayo-


filebis an sarCelze mTlianad an nawilobriv uaris Tqmis Sesaxeb.


mocemul saqmeze saapelacio sasamarTlos daskvnebi da mosazre-


bani aris urTierTsawinaaRmdego, rac SemdegSi mdgomareobs:


mosarCele i. botkoveli sarCeliT moiTxovda sadavo binis 1\2-is


mis sakuTrebad aRiarebas da i. wiklaursa da i. WeliZes Soris dade-


buli nasyidobis xelSekrulebis baTilad cnobas. amasTan, sajaro


reestrs davaleboda sadavo binis 1\2-is registracia mis saxelze.


piris mesakuTred aRiareba niSnavs mis aRiarebas im uflebebis ma-


tareblad, rac nivTis mesakuTres eniWeba: nivTis floba da sargeb-


loba, misi gankargva. Sesabamisad, sasamarTlom aRiara, ra i. botkove-


li sadavo nivTis TanamesakuTred, mas am aRiarebiT mianiWa is ufle-


bebi, rac SeiZleba hqondes nivTis mesakuTres, sajaro reestrSi niv-


Tis TanamesakuTred registraciis uflebis CaTvliT.


amasTan, sasamarTlom mosarCeles uari uTxra nasyidobis xelSek-


rulebis baTilad cnobaze, vinaidan binis myidveli CaTvala keTil-


sindisier SemZenad.

aRniSnuliT sasamarTlom i. WeliZe aseve aRiara sadavo binis mesa-


kuTred Sesabamisi uflebebiT.


raionuli sasamarTlos gadawyvetilebidan gamomdinare, sadavo


farTis mesakuTrea i. WeliZe. amasTan, sadavo farTi warmoadgens sxva


pirTa sakuTrebasac da 1\2-is erT-erTi TanamesakuTre aris i. bot-


kovelic. 


saapelacio sasamarTlom aRniSnuli gadawyvetileba ise datova uc-


vlelad, rom ar gaarkvia, visi ufleba iqna aRiarebuli sadavo nivTze.


saapelacio palata ganmartas, rom sk-is 185-e muxli icavs myidve-


lis qonebriv interesebs, anu garantias iZleva, rom, Tu myidvelma Se-


iZina uZravi nivTi sajaro reestrSi miTiTebuli, am nivTis mesakuTri-


sagan, risTvisac gadauxada mas gansazRvruli Tanxa, igi ar dazaral-


deba, nivTi mas ar CamoerTmeva da aRniSnuli ar SeiZleba iyos damoki-


debuli imaze, moaswro Tu ara myidvelma aRricxva sajaro reestrSi am


nivTis mesakuTred, miT ufro, rodesac, rogorc ukve aRiniSna, es aR-


ricxva ver xerxdeba binaze dadebuli yadaRis gamo. amave ganCinebiT


saapelacio palata aRniSnuli msjelobis sawinaaRmdegod miuTiTebs,


rom sadavo bina unda CaiTvalos meuRleebis: i. botkovelisa da i. wik-


lauris saerTo sakuTrebad da imis gaTvaliswinebiT, rom gadawyveti-


lebis gamotanis momentisaTvis igi teqbiuroSi jer kidev aRricxuli


iyo i. wiklaurze (binaze yadaRis dadebis gamo), sasamarTlom savsebiT


marTebulad aRiara i. botkoveli am binis TanamesakuTred.


sakasacio palata ganmartavs, rom sasamarTlos gadawyvetileba


adgens materialuri samarTlis subieqtebis urTierTdamokidebu-


lebas an sxva samarTlebriv garemoebebs, qmnis uflebis yovelgvari


winaaRmdegobis gareSe realizaciis SesaZleblobebs, aRmofxvris


davas. sasamarTlos gadawyvetilebis sarezolucio nawilidan unda


irkveodes davis Sedegi, kerZod, vis miekuTvna sadavo nivTi, visi uf-


leba iqna aRiarebuli sadavo nivTze. 


gasaCivrebuli gadawyvetilebiT miTiTebuli sakiTxis garkveva


SeuZlebelia.


sk-is 317-e muxlis Tanaxmad, valdebulebis warmoSobisaTvis au-


cilebelia monawileTa Soris xelSekruleba. amave kodeqsis 327-e


muxlis pirveli nawilis Tanaxmad, xelSekruleba dadebulad iTvle-


ba, Tu mxareebi mis yvela arsebiT pirobaze SeTanxmdnen saamisod


gaTvaliswinebuli formiT.


amave kodeqsis 328-e muxlis pirveli nawilis Tanaxmad, Tu kanoniT


xelSekrulebis namdvilobisaTvis dadgenilia gansazRvruli forma


an mxareebma xelSekrulebisaTvis gaiTvaliswines aseTi forma, maSin


xelSekruleba ZalaSi Sedis mxolod am formis Sesaxeb moTxovnis


Sesrulebis Semdeg.


vinaidan mxareebs wiklaursa da WeliZes Soris kanoniT dadgenili


8


formiT gaformda binis nasyidobis xelSekruleba, aRniSnuli xel-


Sekruleba aris ZalaSi.


sk-is 183-e muxlis pirveli nawilis Tanaxmad, uZravi nivTis SesaZe-


nad aucilebelia sanotaro wesiT damowmebuli sabuTi da SemZenis re-


gistracia sajaro reestrSi. sk-is 311-e muxlis pirveli nawilis Tanax-


mad, reestrSi Seitaneba uZrav nivTebze sakuTrebis da sxva sanivTo


uflebebi.aRniSnuli normis Tanaxmad, sajaro reestrSi xdeba ukve ar-


sebuli uflebis Setana. uflebaTa registracia sajaro reestrSi au-


cilebelia kanoniT gansazRvrul SemTxvevebSi da mniSvneloba aqvs sa-


moqalaqo brunvis stabilurobisa da mesame pirTa interesebisaTvis.


sakasacio sasamarTlo Tvlis, rom mocemuli davis gadawyveti-


saTvis mniSvnelovania WeliZesa da wiklaurs Soris gaformebuli


xelSekrulebis namdviloba da ara is, moxda Tu ara misi Semdgomi re-


gistracia sajaro reestrSi. 


sakasacio sasamarTlo iziarebs kasatoris mosazrebas imis Taoba-


ze, rom saapelacio sasamarTlom ar gamoarkvia, meuRleTa mier iyo


SeZenili sadavo qoneba, Tu erT-erTi meuRlis mSoblebma aCuqes maT


es bina, rasac SeiZleba mohyves sxva samarTlebrivi Sedegebi. 


sakasacio palata ganmartavs, rom sk-is 1158-e muxlis Tanaxmad,

da iqnes misi saxlidan, radganac igi ar ixdis binis qiras, amasTan, mas

neuli kasatoris argumenti imis Taobazec, rom mxares sesxis xelSek-


rulebaSi Setanili cvlilebiT daevala procentis procentis gadax-


da. upirveles yovlisa, aseTi garemoeba ar dasturdeba 2003w. 4 Te-


bervlis sesxis xelSekrulebaSi miTiTebuli Tanxis gaangariSebiT


da, agreTve, im garemoebiTac, rom aRniSnuli faqti mxares sadavod


ar gauxdia saapelacio saCivriT.


rac Seexeba im garemoebas, rom b. turabeliZis mier 3000 aSS dola-


ris miReba dasturdeba n.guraspaSvilis mier miRebuli dolarebis


kupiurebis CamonaTvalis qseroasliT, palatis mier gaziarebuli


ver iqneba im safuZvliT, rom aseTi saxis mtkicebuleba wardgenili


ar yofila saqmis arsebiTi ganxilvis dros, xolo sakasacio instan-


cia moklebulia SesaZleblobas, miiRos axali mtkicebulebebi.


saqmis masalebiT arc is garemoeba dasturdeba, rom n.guraspaSvi-


li axdevinebda mas gasesxebuli Tanxis 7%-s. ssk-is 102-e muxlis pir-


veli nawilis Tanaxmad, TiToeulma mxarem unda daamtkicos garemoe-


ba, romelzec igi amyarebs Tavis moTxovnebsa da Sesagebels. sesxis


xelSekrulebaSi procentis odenoba Seadgens 3%-s, xolo procentis


saxiT miRebuli Tanxebis mier dasadasturebel mtkicebulebaze ar


arsebobs gamsesxeblis xelmowerebi, rac SeuZlebels xdis 7%-is


odenobiT msesxeblisaTvis Tanxis gadaxdis faqtis dadgenas.


sk-is 361-e muxlis Sesabamisad, valdebuleba unda Sesruldes je-


rovnad, keTilsindisierad, daTqmul drosa da adgilas. aRniSnuli


normis safuZvelze b.turabeliZe valdebulia, Seasrulos xelSek-


rulebiT nakisri valdebulebani, xolo amave kodeqsis me-300 muxlis


pirveli nawilis Tanaxmad, Tu movale gaaWianurebs im moTxovnis dak-


mayofilebas, romlis uzrunvelyofis saSualebaa ipoTeka, ipoTeka-


ri uflebamosilia, moiTxovos uZravi nivTis realizacia.


zemoaRniSnulidan gamomdinare, palata Tvlis, rom ar arsebobs


saapelacio sasamarTlos mier gamotanili gadawyvetilebis gauqme-


bis safuZveli da igi ucvlelad unda iqnes datovebuli.
